1130        <!-- Shortcuts Samples -->
1131
1132
1133        <!-- This section of sample code shows how your application can add shortcuts to -->
1134        <!-- the launcher (home screen).  Shortcuts have a three step life cycle. -->
1135
1136
1137        <!-- 1.  Your application offers to provide shortcuts to the launcher.  When -->
1138        <!-- the user installs a shortcut, an activity within your application -->
1139        <!-- generates the actual shortcut and returns it to the launcher, where it -->
1140        <!-- is shown to the user as an icon. -->
1141
1142
1143        <!-- 2.  Any time the user clicks on an installed shortcut, an intent is sent. -->
1144        <!-- Typically this would then be handled as necessary by an activity within -->
1145        <!-- your application. -->
1146
1147
1148        <!-- 3.  The shortcut is deleted.  There is no notification to your application. -->
1149
1150
1151        <!-- In order provide shortcuts from your application, you provide three things: -->
1152
1153
1154        <!-- 1.  An intent-filter declaring your ability to provide shortcuts -->
1155        <!-- 2.  Code within the activity to provide the shortcuts as requested -->
1156        <!-- 3.  Code elsewhere within your activity, if appropriate, to receive -->
1157        <!-- intents from the shortcut itself. -->
1158
